Pro Tour Rivals of Ixalan PPTQ Locations
----------------------------------------


Below is the entire list of scheduled Preliminary Pro Tour Qualifiers (PPTQs) that will start you on your path to qualifying for Pro Tour *Rivals of Ixalan*.


The schedule is sorted by date, and then by country. Scroll down to find your country, and you will be able to see all the events taking place in your country. To see your store’s address and contact information, click on the Venue Name. The table is sortable, and you can also use the search box to find a specific store, city, date, or format.


For specific information on PPTQs near you, such as start times and entry fee cost, contact the organizer of the event that you wish to attend.


You can learn more about what events are taking place at your local stores by visiting [locator.wizards.com](file:///C:/Users/toleb/AppData/Local/Microsoft/Windows/Temporary%20Internet%20Files/Content.Outlook/71ZFFH4T/locator.wizards.com).


*Note: the schedule is subject to change. Please contact the store running the event for the most up-to-date information.*


*Triple-asterisks (\*\*\*) denote a change of information since the schedule was initially published.*


*The following goes into an HTML block, and is in the overview section.*


[PPTQs for Pro Tour *Rivals of Ixalan*](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/instoreplay/pptqrix)
